<!-- Update Stock Modal -->
@if (role == "Admin")
{
    <div id="updateStockOverlay" style="display:none;position:fixed;inset:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.45);
             z-index:999;align-items:center;justify-content:center">
        <div style="background:#fff;border-radius:12px;padding:28px;max-width:420px;width:90%;direction:rtl">
            <h4 style="margin:0 0 18px;color:var(--primary);font-size:1rem">
                <i class="fas fa-sync-alt" style="color:var(--secondary)"></i> تحديث الكمية
            </h4>
            <form asp-action="UpdateStock" method="post">
                @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                <input type="hidden" name="inventoryId" value="@Model.InventoryID" />
                <input type="hidden" name="materialId" id="updateMatId" />
                <input type="hidden" id="updateMatFactor" value="0" />
                <div class="form-group">
                    <label>الكمية الجديدة <span style="color:red">*</span></label>
                    <input type="number" name="newQuantity" id="updateNewQty"
                           step="0.001" min="0" class="form-control" required
                           oninput="checkUpdateCapacity()" />
                </div>
                <!-- Update capacity preview -->
                @if (hasCapacity)
                {
                    <div id="updateVolPreview" style="display:none;margin-bottom:10px;padding:9px 12px;
                                 background:#fff3e0;border-radius:7px;font-size:0.83rem;color:#555;border:1px solid #ffe0b2">
                        <i class="fas fa-cube" style="color:#f57c00"></i>
                        الحجم الجديد: <strong id="updateVolVal" style="color:#f57c00"></strong>
                    </div>
                    <div id="updateWarnBox" style="display:none;margin-bottom:10px;padding:10px 14px;
                                 background:#fdecea;border:2px solid #e53935;border-radius:7px;
                                 font-size:0.85rem;color:#b71c1c;font-weight:600">
                        <i class="fas fa-ban"></i> <span id="updateWarnText"></span>
                    </div>
                }
                <div class="form-group">
                    <label>ملاحظات</label>
                    <input type="text" name="notes" class="form-control" placeholder="سبب التعديل..." />
                </div>
                <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;justify-content:flex-end;margin-top:16px">
                    <button type="button" onclick="closeUpdateForm()" class="btn-bonyan-primary">
                        <i class="fas fa-times"></i> إلغاء
                    </button>
                    <button type="submit" id="updateSubmitBtn" class="btn-bonyan-secondary">
                        <i class="fas fa-save"></i> حفظ
                    </button>
                </div>
            </form>
        </div>
    </div>
}

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        // ── Constants passed from server ──────────────────────────
        var REMAINING_CAP = @(hasCapacity? remCap.ToString("F4", System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "-1");
        var TOTAL_CAP = @(hasCapacity? Model.Capacity!.Value.ToString("F4", System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "-1");
        var USED_VOL = @usedVol.ToString("F4", System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);

        // ── Update modal ──────────────────────────────────────────
        var updateMatOtherVolume = 0; // volume of ALL other materials (excluding current one being updated)

        function openUpdateForm(invId, matId, currentQty, matFactor) {
            document.getElementById('updateMatId').value = matId;
            document.getElementById('updateNewQty').value = currentQty;
            document.getElementById('updateMatFactor').value = matFactor;

            // other volume = total used minus current material's volume
            updateMatOtherVolume = USED_VOL - (parseFloat(currentQty) * parseFloat(matFactor));

            document.getElementById('updateStockOverlay').style.display = 'flex';
            checkUpdateCapacity();
        }

        function closeUpdateForm() {
            document.getElementById('updateStockOverlay').style.display = 'none';
        }

        function checkUpdateCapacity() {
            if (TOTAL_CAP < 0) return;
            var qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('updateNewQty').value) || 0;
            var factor = parseFloat(document.getElementById('updateMatFactor').value) || 0;
            var newVol = qty * factor;
            var totalAfter = updateMatOtherVolume + newVol;

            var previewBox = document.getElementById('updateVolPreview');
            var warnBox = document.getElementById('updateWarnBox');
            var warnText = document.getElementById('updateWarnText');
            var submitBtn = document.getElementById('updateSubmitBtn');
            var volVal = document.getElementById('updateVolVal');

            if (qty > 0 && factor > 0) {
                previewBox.style.display = 'block';
                volVal.textContent = newVol.toFixed(2) + ' م³';
            } else {
                previewBox.style.display = 'none';
            }

            if (totalAfter > TOTAL_CAP && TOTAL_CAP > 0) {
                warnBox.style.display = 'block';
                warnText.textContent = 'الكمية المدخلة (' + newVol.toFixed(2) + ' م³) ستتجاوز سعة المخزن! الحد الأقصى المتاح: ' + (TOTAL_CAP - updateMatOtherVolume).toFixed(2) + ' م³';
                submitBtn.disabled = true;
                submitBtn.style.opacity = '0.5';
            } else {
                warnBox.style.display = 'none';
                submitBtn.disabled = false;
                submitBtn.style.opacity = '1';
            }
        }

        // ── Add Material form ─────────────────────────────────────
        function showVolPreview(matSel) {
            var sel = matSel || document.querySelector('select[name="materialId"]');
            var qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('addQty')?.value) || 0;
            var opt = sel?.options[sel?.selectedIndex];
            var factor = parseFloat(opt?.dataset?.factor) || 0;
            var vol = qty * factor;

            var preview = document.getElementById('volPreview');
            var warnBox = document.getElementById('capacityWarnBox');
            var warnText = document.getElementById('capacityWarnText');
            var addBtn = document.getElementById('addMaterialBtn');

            if (qty > 0 && factor > 0) {
                preview.style.display = 'block';
                document.getElementById('volPreviewVal').textContent = vol.toFixed(2) + ' م³';
            } else {
                preview.style.display = 'none';
            }

            // Live capacity enforcement
            if (REMAINING_CAP >= 0 && qty > 0 && factor > 0) {
                if (vol > REMAINING_CAP) {
                    var maxQty = REMAINING_CAP / factor;
                    warnBox.style.display = 'block';
                    warnText.textContent =
                        'الحجم المطلوب (' + vol.toFixed(2) + ' م³) يتجاوز السعة المتبقية (' +
                        REMAINING_CAP.toFixed(2) + ' م³). الحد الأقصى الذي يمكن إضافته: ' +
                        maxQty.toFixed(3) + ' ' + (opt?.dataset?.unit || 'وحدة') + '.';
                    addBtn.disabled = true;
                    addBtn.style.opacity = '0.5';
                } else {
                    warnBox.style.display = 'none';
                    addBtn.disabled = false;
                    addBtn.style.opacity = '1';
                }
            } else {
                warnBox.style.display = 'none';
                if (addBtn) { addBtn.disabled = false; addBtn.style.opacity = '1'; }
            }
        }
    </script>
}=== File: ./BonyanForEngineeringConsultingFirms/Views/Inventory/Edit.cshtml ===

﻿@model Bonyan.DAL.Models.Invoice
@using Bonyan.DAL.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "تفاصيل الفاتورة";
    var role = Context.Session.GetString("Role");

    string statusLabel = Model.Invoice_Status switch
    {
        InvoiceStatus.Paid          => "مدفوعة",
        InvoiceStatus.Unpaid        => "غير مدفوعة",
        InvoiceStatus.PartiallyPaid => "مدفوعة جزئياً",
        _ => Model.Invoice_Status.ToString()
    };
    string statusColor = Model.Invoice_Status switch
    {
        InvoiceStatus.Paid          => "#146c43",
        InvoiceStatus.Unpaid        => "#842029",
        InvoiceStatus.PartiallyPaid => "#7c4a00",
        _ => "#666"
    };
    string statusBg = Model.Invoice_Status switch
    {
        InvoiceStatus.Paid          => "#d1e7dd",
        InvoiceStatus.Unpaid        => "#f8d7da",
        InvoiceStatus.PartiallyPaid => "#fff3cd",
        _ => "#eee"
    };

    decimal net = (Model.Total_Amount ?? 0)
                  * (1 + (Model.Tax ?? 0) / 100)
                  * (1 - (Model.Discount ?? 0) / 100);
}

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        var allSuppliers = [
            @foreach (var s in allSuppliers)
            {
                    @Html.Raw($"{{id:{s.SupplierID},name:'{s.SupplierName.Replace("'", "\\'")}',phone:'{s.Phone ?? ""}',types:'{s.SuppliedMaterialTypes ?? ""}'}},")
            }
        ];

        var volFactors = { Steel: 0.55, Sand: 1.0, Cement: 0.85, Bricks: 1.25, Others: 1.0 };
        var volHints = {
            Steel:  'حديد: 1 طن ≈ 0.55 م³',
            Sand:   'رمل: 1 م³ = 1.0 م³',
            Cement: 'أسمنت: 1 طن ≈ 0.85 م³',
            Bricks: 'طوب: 1000 قطعة ≈ 1.25 م³',
            Others: 'أدخل المعامل المناسب'
        };

        function onMatTypeChange(val) {
            document.getElementById('customNameWrap').style.display = val === 'Others' ? 'block' : 'none';
            document.getElementById('volFactor').value = (volFactors[val] || 1.0).toFixed(4);
            document.getElementById('volHint').textContent = volHints[val] || '';
            renderSuppliers(val);
            updateNotice();
        }

                function renderSuppliers(matType) {
            var container = document.getElementById('supplierContainer');
            document.getElementById('preferredSupplierID').value = '';

            if (!matType) {
                container.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#aaa;font-size:0.88rem;padding:14px;background:#f9f9f9;border-radius:8px;border:1px dashed #ddd"><i class="fas fa-info-circle"></i> اختر نوع المادة أولاً</div>';
                return;
            }

            var matching = allSuppliers.filter(function (s) {
                if (!s.types) return false;
                return s.types.split(',').some(function (t) {
                    t = t.trim();
                    if (matType === 'Others') return t === 'Others' || t.startsWith('Others:');
                    return t === matType;
                });
            });

            if (matching.length === 0) {
                container.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#c62828;font-size:0.88rem;padding:14px;background:#fff3f3;border-radius:8px;border:1px solid #ffcdd2"><i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i> لا يوجد موردون لهذه المادة. يرجى إضافة مورد من صفحة الموردين.</div>';
                return;
            }

            var html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:8px">';
            matching.forEach(function (s) {
                html += '<label class="supplier-card" style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:14px;padding:14px 18px;background:#fff;border:2px solid var(--secondary);border-radius:10px;cursor:pointer;transition:all 0.2s">'
                    + '<input type="radio" name="_supRadio" value="' + s.id + '" onchange="selectSupplier(' + s.id + ',this)" style="width:18px;height:18px;accent-color:var(--primary)">'
                    + '<div><div style="font-weight:700;color:var(--primary);font-size:0.95rem">' + s.name + '</div>'
                    + (s.phone ? '<div style="font-size:0.78rem;color:#888"><i class="fas fa-phone"></i> ' + s.phone + '</div>' : '')
                    + '</div></label>';
            });
            html += '</div>';
            container.innerHTML = html;
        }

        function selectSupplier(id, radio) {
            document.getElementById('preferredSupplierID').value = id;
            document.querySelectorAll('.supplier-card').forEach(function (c) {
                c.style.borderColor = '#e8e8e8';
                c.style.background = '#fff';
            });
            radio.closest('.supplier-card').style.borderColor = 'var(--secondary)';
            radio.closest('.supplier-card').style.background = '#e8f5e9';
            updateNotice();
        }

        function calcTotal() {
            var p = parseFloat(document.getElementById('unitPrice').value) || 0;
            var q = parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 0;
            var t = p * q;
            document.getElementById('totalDisplay').value = t.toFixed(2);
            updateNotice();
            return t;
        }

        function updateNotice() {
            var suppId  = document.getElementById('preferredSupplierID').value;
            var qty     = parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 0;
            var price   = parseFloat(document.getElementById('unitPrice').value) || 0;
            var matType = document.getElementById('matTypeSelect').value;
            var total   = qty * price;
            var notice  = document.getElementById('invoiceNotice');
            if (suppId && qty > 0 && price > 0 && matType) {
                notice.style.display = 'block';
                document.getElementById('notMat').textContent   = matType;
                document.getElementById('notCalc').textContent  = qty.toFixed(3) + ' × ' + price.toFixed(2) + ' ج.م';
                document.getElementById('notTotal').textContent = total.toFixed(2) + ' ج.م';
            } else {
                notice.style.display = 'none';
            }
        }

        function beforeSubmit() {
            var matType = document.getElementById('matTypeSelect').value;
            if (matType === 'Others') {
                var custom = document.getElementById('customName').value.trim();
                if (!custom) { alert('يرجى كتابة اسم المادة الأخرى'); return false; }
                document.getElementById('matTypeSelect').value = custom;
            }
            return true;
        }
    </script>

                        Bonyan.DAL.Enums.MaterialTaskStatus.Delivered => "تم التسليم",
                        _ => mt.Status.ToString()
                    };
                    string statusClass = mt.Status switch
                    {
                        Bonyan.DAL.Enums.MaterialTaskStatus.Requested => "badge-pending",
                        Bonyan.DAL.Enums.MaterialTaskStatus.Approved => "badge-inprogress",
                        Bonyan.DAL.Enums.MaterialTaskStatus.Delivered => "badge-completed",
                        _ => ""
                    };
                    <tr>
                        <td>@(mt.Task?.Task_Name ?? "—")</td>
                        <td>@(mt.Task?.Project?.ProjectName ?? "—")</td>
                        <td>@mt.QuantityRequired.ToString("N2")</td>
                        <td>@(mt.QuantityUsed.HasValue? mt.QuantityUsed.Value.ToString("N2") : "—")</td>
                        <td><span class="task-status-badge @statusClass">@statusLabel</span></td>
                        <td>@mt.RequestDate.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")</td>
                    </tr>
                }
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>
}

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        function calcTotal() {
            var price = parseFloat(document.getElementById('unitPrice').value) || 0;
            var qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('quantity').value) || 0;
            document.getElementById('totalAmount').value = (price * qty).toFixed(2);
        }
    </script>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        // ── Supplier loader via AJAX ───────────────────────────────
        var materialSelect = document.getElementById('materialSelect');
        var supplierSelect = document.getElementById('supplierSelect');
        var supplierHint   = document.getElementById('supplierHint');

        if (materialSelect) {
            materialSelect.addEventListener('change', function () {
                var matId = this.value;

                supplierSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- جاري التحميل... --</option>';
                if (supplierHint) supplierHint.style.display = 'none';

                if (!matId) {
                    supplierSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- اختر المادة أولاً --</option>';
                    calcFinal();
                    return;
                }

                fetch('/MaterialInvoice/GetSuppliersForMaterial?materialId=' + matId)
                    .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
                    .then(function (data) {
                        supplierSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- اختر المورد --</option>';
                        if (data.length === 0) {
                            if (supplierHint) supplierHint.style.display = 'block';
                        } else {
                            data.forEach(function (s) {
                                var opt = document.createElement('option');
                                opt.value = s.supplierID;
                                opt.textContent = s.supplierName;
                                supplierSelect.appendChild(opt);
                            });
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(function () {
                        supplierSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- خطأ في تحميل الموردين --</option>';
                    });

                // auto-fill unit price and quantity from data attributes
                var selected = materialSelect.options[materialSelect.selectedIndex];
                var price    = selected ? selected.getAttribute('data-price') : null;
                var qty      = selected ? selected.getAttribute('data-qty')   : null;
                var priceEl  = document.querySelector('[name="UnitPrice"]');
                var qtyEl    = document.querySelector('[name="Quantity"]');
                if (priceEl && price) priceEl.value = price;
                if (qtyEl   && qty)   qtyEl.value   = qty;

                calcFinal();
            });
        }

        // ── Calculation ───────────────────────────────────────────
        function calcFinal() {
            var qty      = parseFloat(document.querySelector('[name="Quantity"]')?.value)        || 0;
            var price    = parseFloat(document.querySelector('[name="UnitPrice"]')?.value)       || 0;
            var tax      = parseFloat(document.getElementById('TaxPercent')?.value)     || 0;
            var discount = parseFloat(document.getElementById('DiscountPercent')?.value) || 0;

            var total   = qty * price;
            var taxAmt  = total * tax / 100;
            var discAmt = total * discount / 100;
            var final   = total + taxAmt - discAmt;

            var setEl = function (id, val) {
                var el = document.getElementById(id);
                if (el) el.textContent = val.toFixed(2) + ' ج.م';
            };
            setEl('dispTotal', total);
            setEl('dispTax',   taxAmt);
            setEl('dispDisc',  discAmt);
            setEl('dispFinal', final);
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', calcFinal);

        // ── Cancel modal ──────────────────────────────────────────
        function confirmCancelInvoice() {
            document.getElementById('cancelModal').classList.add('active');
        }
        function closeCancelModal() {
            document.getElementById('cancelModal').classList.remove('active');
        }
    </script>

            var price = parseFloat(document.getElementById('unitPrice').value) || 0;
            var taxPct = parseFloat(document.getElementById('tax').value) || 0;

            var taxAmt = total * taxPct / 100;

            var final = total + taxAmt - discAmt;
            document.getElementById('dispTotal').textContent = total.toFixed(2) + ' ج.م';
            document.getElementById('dispTax').textContent = taxAmt.toFixed(2) + ' ج.م';
            document.getElementById('dispDisc').textContent = discAmt.toFixed(2) + ' ج.م';
            document.getElementById('dispFinal').textContent = final.toFixed(2) + ' ج.م';
        }
        calcAll();
    </script>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        function toggleEmpDropdown() {
            const panel   = document.getElementById('empDropdownPanel');
            const chevron = document.getElementById('empChevron');
            const isOpen  = panel.style.display === 'block';
            panel.style.display        = isOpen ? 'none' : 'block';
            chevron.style.transform    = isOpen ? 'rotate(0deg)' : 'rotate(180deg)';
        }

        function updateEmpLabel() {
            const checked = document.querySelectorAll(
                'input[name="selectedEmployees"]:checked');
            const label = document.getElementById('empDropdownLabel');
            if (checked.length === 0) {
                label.textContent = '-- اختر المهندسين --';
            } else {
                label.textContent = Array.from(checked)
                    .map(cb => cb.getAttribute('data-name'))
                    .join('، ');
            }
        }

        // Close when clicking outside
        document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
            const btn   = document.getElementById('empDropdownBtn');
            const panel = document.getElementById('empDropdownPanel');
            if (btn && panel &&
                !btn.contains(e.target) &&
                !panel.contains(e.target)) {
                panel.style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('empChevron')
                         .style.transform = 'rotate(0deg)';
            }
        });
    </script>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        function showTab(tabId) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel')
                    .forEach(p => p.style.display = 'none');
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn')
                    .forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active-tab'));
            document.getElementById(tabId).style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('btn-' + tabId).classList.add('active-tab');
        }
    </script>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        function filterProjects() {
            const search = document.getElementById('searchInput')
                                   .value.toLowerCase();
            const status = document.getElementById('statusFilter')
                                   .value.toLowerCase();
            const cards  = document.querySelectorAll('.project-card');

            cards.forEach(card => {
                const name      = card.getAttribute('data-name') || '';
                const cardStatus = card.getAttribute('data-status') || '';

                const matchSearch = name.includes(search);
                const matchStatus = status === '' || cardStatus === status;

                card.style.display = (matchSearch && matchStatus) ? '' : 'none';
            });
        }
    </script>

﻿@model Bonyan.DAL.Models.SiteVisit
@using Bonyan.DAL.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "تفاصيل زيارة الموقع";
    var role = Context.Session.GetString("Role");
    string safetyLabel = Model.SafetyStatus switch
    {
        SafetyStatus.Safe => "آمن",
        SafetyStatus.NeedAttention => "يحتاج انتباه",
        SafetyStatus.Critical => "حرج",
        _ => Model.SafetyStatus.ToString()
    };
    string safetyClass = Model.SafetyStatus switch
    {
        SafetyStatus.Safe => "badge-safe",
        SafetyStatus.NeedAttention => "badge-attention",
        SafetyStatus.Critical => "badge-critical",
        _ => ""
    };
}

<link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/sitevisit.css" />

    <div class="page-header-left">
        <h2><i class="fas fa-hard-hat" style="color:var(--secondary)"></i> تفاصيل زيارة الموقع</h2>
    </div>
    <div style="display:flex; gap:10px">
        <a asp-controller="Project" asp-action="Details" asp-route-id="@Model.ProjId" class="btn-bonyan-primary">
            <i class="fas fa-arrow-right"></i> رجوع للمشروع
        </a>
        @if (role == "Admin")
        {
            <a asp-action="Edit" asp-route-id="@Model.VisitId" class="btn-bonyan-secondary">
                <i class="fas fa-edit"></i> تعديل
            </a>
        }
    </div>
</div>

        </h3>

        await Html.RenderPartialAsync("_ValidationScriptsPartial");

    <script>
        function previewImage(input) {
            if (input.files && input.files[0]) {
                const reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = e => {
                    const img = document.getElementById('imgPreview');
                    img.src = e.target.result;
                    img.style.display = 'block';
                    document.getElementById('dropContent').style.display = 'none';
                    document.getElementById('dropZone').style.borderColor = 'var(--secondary)';
                };
                reader.readAsDataURL(input.files[0]);
            }
        }
        const zone = document.getElementById('dropZone');
        zone.addEventListener('dragover',  e => { e.preventDefault(); zone.classList.add('dragover'); });
        zone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => zone.classList.remove('dragover'));
        zone.addEventListener('drop', e => {
            e.preventDefault(); zone.classList.remove('dragover');
            if (e.dataTransfer.files.length) {
                document.getElementById('fileInput').files = e.dataTransfer.files;
                previewImage(document.getElementById('fileInput'));
            }
        });
    </script>

<style>
    .mat-chip {
        display: inline-flex;
        align-items: center;
        gap: 6px;
        padding: 5px 14px;
        border-radius: 20px;
        font-size: 0.82rem;
        font-weight: 600;
        color: #fff
    }

    .chip-Steel {
        background: #546e7a
    }

    .chip-Sand {
        background: #fb8c00
    }

    .chip-Cement {
        background: #78909c;
        color: #222
    }

    .chip-Bricks {
        background: #e53935
    }

    .chip-Others {
        background: #8e24aa
    }

    #dropdownToggle:hover {
        border-color: var(--primary)
    }
</style>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        var chipLabels={Steel:'حديد (Steel)',Sand:'رمل (Sand)',Cement:'أسمنت (Cement)',Bricks:'طوب (Bricks)',Others:'أخرى'};

        function toggleDropdown(){
            var d=document.getElementById('materialDropdown');
            var a=document.getElementById('dropdownArrow');
            var open=d.style.display==='block';
            d.style.display=open?'none':'block';
            a.style.transform=open?'rotate(0deg)':'rotate(180deg)';
            document.getElementById('dropdownToggle').style.borderColor=open?'#e0e0e0':'var(--primary)';
        }

        document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
            var btn=document.getElementById('dropdownToggle');
            var dd=document.getElementById('materialDropdown');
            if(btn&&dd&&!btn.contains(e.target)&&!dd.contains(e.target)){
                dd.style.display='none';
                document.getElementById('dropdownArrow').style.transform='rotate(0deg)';
                document.getElementById('dropdownToggle').style.borderColor='#e0e0e0';
            }
        });

        function onTypeChange(type){
            var cb=document.getElementById('chk_'+type);
            var lbl=document.getElementById('lbl_'+type);
            lbl.style.background=cb.checked?'#f0f7ff':'#fff';
            if(type==='Others'){
                document.getElementById('othersBox').style.display=cb.checked?'block':'none';
                if(!cb.checked) document.getElementById('othersText').value='';
            }
            updateChips();
            updateLabel();
        }

        function updateChips(){
            var c=document.getElementById('selectedChips');
            c.innerHTML='';
            document.querySelectorAll('.mat-type-cb:checked').forEach(function(cb){
                var t=cb.value;
                var text=t==='Others'?'أخرى: '+(document.getElementById('othersText').value||'...')
                                      :chipLabels[t];
                var span=document.createElement('span');
                span.className='mat-chip chip-'+t;
                span.innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> '+text;
                c.appendChild(span);
            });
        }

        function updateLabel(){
            var checked=document.querySelectorAll('.mat-type-cb:checked');
            var lbl=document.getElementById('dropdownLabel');
            if(checked.length===0){
                lbl.textContent='— اختر المواد التي يورّدها —';
                lbl.style.color='#aaa';
            }else{
                lbl.textContent=checked.length+' '+(checked.length===1?'مادة':'مواد')+' محددة';
                lbl.style.color='var(--primary)';
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('othersText').addEventListener('input',updateChips);
    </script>

    ViewData["Title"] = "تعديل مورد";
    var materialTypes = new[] { "Steel", "Sand", "Cement", "Bricks", "Others" };
    var materialLabels = new Dictionary<string, string> {
        {"Steel","حديد (Steel)"},{"Sand","رمل (Sand)"},
        {"Cement","أسمنت (Cement)"},{"Bricks","طوب (Bricks)"},{"Others","أخرى (Others)"}
    };
    // Parse existing types
    var existingTypes = (Model.SuppliedMaterialTypes ?? "")
        .Split(',', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries).ToList();
    var checkedTypes = existingTypes.Select(t => t.StartsWith("Others:") ? "Others" : t).ToList();
    var othersValue = existingTypes.FirstOrDefault(t => t.StartsWith("Others:"))?.Substring(7) ?? "";
}

                    <div id="materialDropdown"
                         style="display:none;position:absolute;top:calc(100% + 4px);right:0;left:0;

                                box-shadow:0 4px 16px rgba(0,0,0,0.12);z-index:100;overflow:hidden">
                        @foreach (var type in materialTypes)
                        {
                            bool isChecked2 = checkedTypes.Contains(type);
                            <label id="label_@type"
                                   style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;padding:12px 16px;

                                              background:@(isChecked2 ? "#e8f5e9" : "#fff");

                                <input type="checkbox" name="selectedMaterialTypes" value="@type"
                                       id="chk_@type" class="mat-type-cb"

<style>
    .mat-chip {
        display: inline-flex;
        align-items: center;
        gap: 6px;
        background: var(--primary);
        color: #fff;
        padding: 4px 12px;
        border-radius: 20px;
        font-size: 0.82rem;
        font-weight: 600;
    }

        .mat-chip.others {
            background: #ab47bc;
        }

        .mat-chip.steel {
            background: #607d8b;
        }

        .mat-chip.sand {
            background: #ffa726;
        }

        .mat-chip.cement {
            background: #90a4ae;
            color: #333;
        }

        .mat-chip.bricks {
            background: #ef5350;
        }
</style>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const labels = { Steel:'حديد (Steel)', Sand:'رمل (Sand)', Cement:'أسمنت (Cement)', Bricks:'طوب (Bricks)', Others:'أخرى' };
        const chipClass = { Steel:'steel', Sand:'sand', Cement:'cement', Bricks:'bricks', Others:'others' };

        function toggleDropdown() {
            var d = document.getElementById('materialDropdown');
            var a = document.getElementById('dropdownArrow');
            var open = d.style.display === 'block';
            d.style.display = open ? 'none' : 'block';
            a.style.transform = open ? 'rotate(0deg)' : 'rotate(180deg)';
        }
        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (!document.getElementById('dropdownToggle').contains(e.target) &&
                !document.getElementById('materialDropdown').contains(e.target)) {
                document.getElementById('materialDropdown').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('dropdownArrow').style.transform = 'rotate(0deg)';
            }
        });
        function isChecked(type) { return document.getElementById('chk_' + type)?.checked; }
        function onTypeChange(type) {
            var cb = document.getElementById('chk_' + type);
            document.getElementById('label_' + type).style.background = cb.checked ? '#e8f5e9' : '#fff';
            if (type === 'Others') {
                document.getElementById('othersBox').style.display = cb.checked ? 'block' : 'none';
                if (!cb.checked) document.getElementById('othersText').value = '';
            }
            updateChips(); updateDropdownLabel();
        }
        function updateChips() {
            var c = document.getElementById('selectedChips');
            c.innerHTML = '';
            document.querySelectorAll('.mat-type-cb:checked').forEach(function(cb) {
                var type = cb.value;
                var text = type === 'Others' ? 'أخرى: ' + (document.getElementById('othersText').value || '...') : labels[type];
                var chip = document.createElement('span');
                chip.className = 'mat-chip ' + (chipClass[type] || '');
                chip.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> ' + text;
                c.appendChild(chip);
            });
        }
        function updateDropdownLabel() {
            var checked = document.querySelectorAll('.mat-type-cb:checked');
            var lbl = document.getElementById('dropdownLabel');
            lbl.textContent = checked.length === 0 ? '-- اختر المواد المورَّدة --' : checked.length + ' مادة محددة';
            lbl.style.color = checked.length === 0 ? '#888' : 'var(--primary)';
        }
        document.getElementById('othersText')?.addEventListener('input', updateChips);
        // Initialize chips on page load
        updateChips();
    </script>
}=== File: ./BonyanForEngineeringConsultingFirms/Views/Supplier/Index.cshtml ===

﻿@model Bonyan.DAL.Models.Task
@using Bonyan.DAL.Enums

    };

@section Scripts {
    <script type="text/javascript">
        function filterTasksByProject(projId) {
            if (projId) {
                window.location.href = '@Url.Action("Index", "Task")?projectId=' + projId;
            } else {
                window.location.href = '@Url.Action("Index", "Task")';
            }
        }
    </script>
